**causa 1.कारण** *n.,***हेतु** *m.***2.***Law***वाद** *m.***3.***Logic* **कारण** *n.*  
**causaaequat effectum कारणं कार्येण समम्, कार्यकारणे समे  
causa causae est causa causati कारणस्यकारणंकार्यस्य**

**कारणम्, कारण-कारणं कार्यकारणम्**  

**causa causans 1.**(cause in action) **कार्ये कारणम् 2.**(immediate cause as opposed to a remote

cause)

**अनन्तर कारण**

**causa causata कारणस्य कारणम्  
causa cognoscendi ज्ञानस्य कारणम्  
causa effeciens** (efficient cause) **निमित्त-कारण** (ancient word)  
**causa eminens** (a cause transcending its effect) **अतिरोही कारण  
causa essendi** (cause of being) **अस्ति-कारण  
causa fiendi** (cause ofbecoming) **भवति-कारण  
causa finalis** (final cause) **अन्तिम कारण  
causa impotentiae** (by reason of impotence— Aiyar p-182a) **क्लीबता के कारण  
causal** *adj. Logic* **1.**(expressing a cause)**कारणवाची** (-इन्)

**2.**(relating to a cause) **कारण-संबद्ध 3.**

(containing acause) **कारण-युत 4.**(of the nature of a cause) **कारण-रूप**

**causa latet, visest notissima कारणम् अदृश्यं, दृश्यं कार्यम्  
causal influence** *Bot.* **कारणभूत प्रभाव

**कारणता***f.,*

**कारणत्व**

*n.*

(ancient words)

**causa mortis मृत्यु-कारणात्, मृत्यु के कारण

**causatum** *Logic* **कार्य** *n.*  
**causa turpis** *Law*(an unlawful motive or purpose) **अवैध प्रेरणा  
cause 1.कारण** *n.,***हेतु** *m.***,निमित्त** *n.***2.विचार्य पद** *n.*

**3.**(side of a question) **पक्ष** *m.***4.***Law* **वाद** *m.*

(Const.)

**accidental cause असमवायी कारण  
artificial cause कृत्रिम कारण  
efficient** *or* **moving cause** (as labour) **कर्तृ-कारण**  
**final cause** (as the completed house) **अन्तिमकारण  
first cause** (the divine mind) **आदि कारण  
formal cause** (as the form of a house in the mind of the builder) **रूप-कारण  
material cause** (as bricks, timber, etc.) **द्रव्य-कारण**  
**natural cause प्राकृत कारण  
plurality of causes कारण-बहुत्व  
without due cause यथोचित कारण के बिना  
without good cause समुचित कारण के बिना**

**cause** *vb.* **करवाना

cause and fact** *Statistics* **कारण और तथ्य

**crop 1.**(harvest) **सस्य** *n.*, **फसल 2.**(a pouchlike enlargement of the gullet of many birds, serving

as a receptacle for food) **गलधानिका ** *f.*, **अन्नग्रह** *m.* **3.***Forestry* **सस्य, वन** *n.,* **उपज**

**⇒Forest crops are sometimes classified in terms of their stages of development thus:**  

**seedling crop** (from the germination of the seed till the time when the plants reach 3' in height) **नव-पादप-सस्य, नवपादप-वन**  

**thicket** *or* **sapling crop** (from the time when the young trees reach 3in height till the lower branches begin to fall) **बालवृक्ष-सस्य, बालवृक्ष-वन**  

**pole crop** (from the fall of the lower branches to the time when the rate of increase in height begins to fall off and crown expansion becomes marked) **वृक्षक-सस्य, वृक्षक-वन  
tree crop** (when it has passed the pole stage) **वृक्ष-सस्य, वृक्ष-वन** (I.F.R. p.6)
